name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Superior Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:17 Reviews
rating:3.7
posted:Posted April 8, 2024
msg:I stayed here for 3 nights during the Qingming Festival in 2024.

In terms of location, it was close to Bayi Square and was a perfect place for sightseeing in the area.

It is a 3-minute walk from Ding Park South on subway line 2, so I recommend using the subway.

It is a 5-star hotel, but it was renovated in 2016, so it is 8 years old, and unlike recent hotels, it still feels old.

However, it is well cleaned, so it is clean.

Since the floor is carpeted, I asked for a non-smoking room because many people are concerned about the smell.

All rooms have a bathtub and I did not use the shower, but there is no problem with the amount of hot water.

Basic amenities, 2 free plastic bottles, TV, refrigerator, all at a standard level.

The impression/attitude of the staff is also fine.

As for breakfast, first of all, it starts at 7:00, but it is not ready until after 7:30.

It is 30 minutes, but I wish they would try harder. Also, the quality of the food is not good. There are Nanchang local dishes every day, but there are very few other menus. The congee/baozi etc. are normal, but the fried rice/fried noodles
are not that great. Therefore, I ate bread/cakes ordered from elsewhere.
I wish they would make a bit more effort!
As for dinner, there aren't many big restaurants nearby, just ramen/hamburger places,
so it might be better to eat around the tourist spots.

As mentioned above, it does feel old, but in terms of cost-effectiveness, it's a good choice for tourists, so I recommend it!
----------------------------------------
